Source: seed-images.js

// SEED PATTERN IMAGES
// =============================================================================
// Embeds sample coin images as CUSTOM pattern rules for first-time user demo.
// On first run, creates two custom Numista lookup rules (American Silver Eagle
// and Canadian Gold Maple Leaf) with real coin photos so new users can see how
// to edit, delete, and export pattern images without uploading anything first.
//
// Images are loaded into IndexedDB on first run via imageCache.cachePatternImage().
// Rules are created via NumistaLookup.addRule(). Both appear in
// Settings > Images > Custom Pattern Rules where users can interact with them.
//
// To update images, replace the base64 data URIs and bump SEED_IMAGES_VERSION.
// =============================================================================

/**
 * Version string for seed images. Bump when images are updated so existing
 * caches get refreshed. Stored in localStorage as 'seedImagesVer'.
 * @constant {string}
 */
const SEED_IMAGES_VERSION = '1';

/**
 * Seed custom rule definitions with embedded base64 WebP image data.
 * Each entry becomes a custom pattern rule in NumistaLookup, visible in
 * Settings > Images > Custom Pattern Rules with thumbnails.
 *
 * @type {Array<{pattern: string, replacement: string, numistaId: string|null, obverse: string, reverse: string}>}
 */

/**
 * Converts a data URI string to a Blob.
 * @param {string} dataUri - Full data URI (e.g. "data:image/webp;base64,...")
 * @returns {Blob}
 */
const dataUriToBlob = (dataUri) => {
  const [header, base64] = dataUri.split(',');
  const mime = header.match(/:(.*?);/)[1];
  const binary = atob(base64);
  const bytes = new Uint8Array(binary.length);
  for (let i = 0; i < binary.length; i++) {
    bytes[i] = binary.charCodeAt(i);
  }
  return new Blob([bytes], { type: mime });
};

/**
 * Loads seed pattern images as custom rules into NumistaLookup + IndexedDB.
 * Creates two demo custom pattern rules with real coin photos for first-time
 * users. Skips if already loaded at current version.
 */
const loadSeedImages = async () => {
  // Guard: both imageCache and NumistaLookup must be available
  if (typeof imageCache === 'undefined' || !imageCache.isAvailable()) return;
  if (typeof NumistaLookup === 'undefined' || !NumistaLookup.addRule) return;

  // Check version  skip if already loaded at this version
  const storedVer = localStorage.getItem('seedImagesVer');
  if (storedVer === SEED_IMAGES_VERSION) return;

  debugLog('[SeedImages] Loading seed custom pattern rules (v' + SEED_IMAGES_VERSION + ')...');
  let loaded = 0;

  for (let i = 0; i < SEED_CUSTOM_RULES.length; i++) {
    const entry = SEED_CUSTOM_RULES[i];
    if (!entry.obverse && !entry.reverse) continue;

    try {
      // Generate a deterministic seedImageId for the cached image
      const seedImageId = 'seed-custom-img-' + i;

      // Create the custom pattern rule (links to seedImageId for image lookup)
      const result = NumistaLookup.addRule(
        entry.pattern,
        entry.replacement,
        entry.numistaId,
        seedImageId
      );

      if (!result.success) {
        console.warn('[SeedImages] Failed to add rule "' + entry.pattern + '":', result.error);
        continue;
      }

      // Cache obverse/reverse images in IndexedDB
      const obvBlob = entry.obverse ? dataUriToBlob(entry.obverse) : null;
      const revBlob = entry.reverse ? dataUriToBlob(entry.reverse) : null;
      await imageCache.cachePatternImage(seedImageId, obvBlob, revBlob);

      loaded++;
      debugLog('[SeedImages] Created rule + cached images: ' + entry.pattern);
    } catch (e) {
      console.warn('[SeedImages] Failed to load seed rule "' + entry.pattern + '":', e);
    }
  }

  // Mark version as loaded (even if 0 loaded  prevents retry on rules that were deleted)
  try {
    localStorage.setItem('seedImagesVer', SEED_IMAGES_VERSION);
  } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }

  debugLog('[SeedImages] Done. Loaded ' + loaded + ' seed custom pattern rules.');
};

// Expose globally
if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {
  window.loadSeedImages = loadSeedImages;
}
